 jis vajah se mayawati ne sirf do siton kaa vaada kiya he
 Ansari Brothers will fight from here, Ansari brothers are expected to contest from Mohammadabad of Gazipur and Sadar seat of Mau
 mau sadar kii seat se bahubali mukhtaar ansaari vidhayak hai to mohammadabad seat se unke bhai sibgatullah ansaari vidhayak hai
 BSP had earlier nominated Manoj Rai from Sadar seat of Mau and Vinod Rai from Mohammadabad seat
 sapa or congress gathbandhan se ho rahe nuksaan ko kam karne kii kavaidaupi chunaav main philvakt sabase adhik maaramaari muslim voton ko lekar ho rahi he
 While the SP and Congress have formed an alliance to support Muslim voters, on the other hand, the BSP has already put its claim on this vote bank by taking down 97 Muslim candidates 
 purvanchal main muslimon ke bade netaa maane jane vaale mukhtaar ansaari ke parivaar ke basapa main jane se muslim votaron kaa jhukaav bispi kii taraf ho saktaa he
 BSP supremo Mayawati has made preparations to give tickets to Ansari brothers by cutting two tickets under this strategy
 muslim vot kii jimmedaari in kandhon parmuslim vot saadhane kii jimmedaari bispi ne apane mahasachiv nasimuddin siddiki ko de rakhi he
 Siddiqui has been given the responsibility of western Uttar Pradesh where he is continuously holding rallies and meetings
 siddiki ke alaava mayawati ne saansad munkad ali, naushaad ali or atahar khan ko muslim morche par aage kiya he
 Munkad Ali is promoting the BSP in Varanasi, Allahabad and Mirzapur divisions, while Naushad Ali is assigned to Bundelkhand and Athar Khan to Faizabad and Devipatan division
 dilli ke south east jile ke nivaasiyon ne timarpur-okhla west menagement company ( west tu energy plant, okhla) prastaavit pariyojna ko 16 mega wat se 40 megawatt karne ke khilaaf saikadon log sadak par utre
 These people made the first human chain by taking to the streets from 12 to 2 am on Sunday and after leaving Sukhdev Vihar reached different areas and raised their voice
 is human chen main prabhavit ilaake sukhdev vihaar, jasola , gaffaar manzil, haji colony, johri form, okhla vihaar, shaheen baag, abul fazal inkalev , batla house, messehgarh, badarpur, madanpur khadar tathaa dilli ke anya rihaayshi ilaakon se saikadon kii sankhya main logon ne maanav shrinkhalaa banaaya
 After this these people also performed
 gauratlab he ki plant ko 40 megawatt karne se lagbhag 40 lakh logon ke prabhavit hone ki ashankahai
 a special report was also published by NDTV Khabar on 19 January 2019 in this regard
 jan andolanon kaa rashtriya samanvay kanvinar vimal bhai ne enditivi se bataaya ki prashn kai he, 16 megawatt kii upji samasya kaa samaadhaan nahi? sarkarein 40 kii baat kaise kar sakati hai?dilli pradooshan niyantran board andeh ke ghere main he
 Why doesn't he make his surveillance report public? How is this plant operating in a population of millions and in the green belt? The government cannot avoid these questions by calling it the best disposal of Kachri
 ardblue jasola hits adhyaksh shakeel ahamed ne enditivi ko bataaya ki yah maanav shrankhla sukhdev vihaar se lage hue kooday se bijli banane vaale jindal company ke 16 megawatt plant or usko 40 megawatt main tabdili kii koshish ke khilaaf yojit kii gai thi
 The administration and pollution control board had to cancel the public hearing organized for this expansion on January 16 due to the huge outrage among the people
 16 megawatt plant ke khilaaf supreme court main cese chal rahaa he phir ise 40 megawatt karne kii itani jaldi kyon?human chaiyn main maujuud buniyaad ( enjio ) adhyaksha gazala hashmi evam samajasevi vakil johari ,parvaiz khan kehete he ki paryaavarniya jansunwaayee ek atyant mahatvapurn sanvaidhanik adhikaar he jahaan log apni baat rakh pate hai isliye jab 16 megawatt kii pariyojna ko aage badha kar 40 megawatt karne karnaa janata ko maut ke bich kheenchna he , jo maanavadhikaar kaa ullaghan heki bure asar ko dur nahin kiya gaya or naa hi is bare main koi gambhir pahal najar aati he, tab atirikt 24 megawatt badhaane ke kya dushprinaam honge?kya kabhi ye akalan kiya gaya kii harith pattee hone v itani ghani aabaadi ke bich is plant kyon rakhaa gaya ? vahiin, okhla ke samajasevi mohammad umr khan or shakeel ur rahamaan khan kehete he prabhavit logo ne shanti purvak human chaiyn kaa aayojan karke dilli sarkaar ko sidhi chetavanee di he ki agar kejariwal sarkaar ne is ore koi thos kadam nahin uthaaya to chunaav main khamyaaza bhugatne ke liye taiyaar rahen
 Because the Delhi government is directly supporting those who play with our lives
 soshal pride welfare socity adhyaksh doctor kamaal auki afazal ansaari kehete he ki aakhir harith pattee viksit karne ke naam par hariyaali ko jalaane vaala plant yahaan sthapit kiya gaya

 2020 main relies hone vaali is film ke jariye bhartiya cricket team ke pehla world cap jeetne ke sanrghash or uski kahani ko dikhaaya jayega
 The Seventh Pay Commission has reduced the minimum wage of regular employees in the country to 18,000, but the workers working in Prime Minister Narendra Modi's own state of Gujarat, contracted, are forced to work at a much lower salary
 in karmchaariyon ke liye sarkari karmchaariyon ke baraabar vetan paanaa abhi tak sapana hi bana hua he
 More than 6000 sanitation workers of Ahmedabad have been on strike for more than a week on this demand for increase in salary
 unka kahana he ki kai logon kii phulatime bhartee bahut pehle ho gai lekin sarkaar unhen bilkul tavajjo nahin de rahi
 Their condition is bad because of the contract system
 lambii ladaai ke baad sarkaar ne unhen do saal pehle hi sarkari kontract par rakhaa he jo kabhi bhi radd ho saktaa he
 These people are left as daily wage laborers
 inhen ravivaar ko bhi chuttee nahin milti
 Not only this, if he fell ill, then that day's money went
 narendra modi desh ke pradhanmantri ho gaye hai lekin gujarat ke mukhyamantri rahete unhone jo nitiyaan banaain, unase karmchaaree aaj bhi khafa hai
 Even an employee named Gitaben Rathore says that she hardly gets 7000 to 8000 rupees every month
 ye bhi pichley 15 saal se zyada se kaam karne ke baad
 They live in a rented house, pay 3-4 thousand rent, get their children educated to fill their stomach
 inhen na medical miltaa he na ravivaar kii chuttee
 Not only this, even if someone dies in the house, there is also the possibility of getting a salary cut
 ahmedabad municipal korporation ke malaria vibhaag main kaam kar rahe natvarbhai bhi pichley ek saptaah se hadtaal par hai
 He complains that despite a 20-year job, he is not on regular basis, is on contract
 vetan kul milakar 9300 miltaa he
 In the rainy season, malaria is sprayed in the affected areas in the morning and evening but there is no insurance for health
 malaria vibhaag main 200 se zyaada pad pichley kareeb 10 saal se khaali hai
 But people like him are being exploited in the name of contract
 vashishtha sharma safaai karmchaaree nahin, shikshak hai
 Not a teacher, education assistant
 gujarat sarkaar apane shikshakon ko darasal yahi darja detii he
 Fixes in salary for five years on contract
 iske baad hi puure shikshak kii selary mil paati he
 Vashisht Sharma, who teaches chemistry in Higher Secondary, does not understand this 'mystery' of different salary for the same work
 sharma kehete hai ki ve lagaataar rojgari or nunatam tankhwaah ke muddon par mukhyamantri, pradhanmantri sabaki baaten sunate hai, jinka daawa he ki desh bhi bahut aage bad gaya he
 But it is also difficult to run the house of Gujarat teacher or government employee, who falls in the third-fourth category
 ve bataate hai ki maan lijie yah15,000 bhi ho to ghar kaise chalegaa
 If they want to take some loan, then the bank says that at least 15,000 rupees should be paid, if they go to take 10 thousand loans then they cannot get it either
 gujarat main 1996 main praathmik shikshakon ke liye baalguru yojana main sarkaar ne pehali baar tankhwaah fiks kii
 But for the first time in 2006, a policy of fixed salary was made in Gujarat after Narendra Modi became the Chief Minister
 iske daayre main kai pad aa gaye
 In 2006, salaries for most posts were fixed at Rs 2500 per month
 kuch padon ke liye yah 4500 rupye thi
 Despite heavy opposition, this salary continued for five years, the salary was increased from 2500 in 2011 to 4500 and in 2012 to 5300 rupees
 sarkaar kii is niti ke kilaaf kanoonee or andolan ke zarie ladaai ghad rahe jan adhikaar manch ke ram praveen kehete hai ki teen tarah se bhartiyon ho rahi hai or teenon main shoshan he
 Police holds fix salary for 5 years on posts like constable, sub inspector, teacher, patwari
 ye paanch saal na unki naukari main gine jate hai na inhen koi or sarkari laabh miltaa he
 Neither is the benefit of seniority
 is darmiyaan lambii chuttee bhi nahin lee ja sakati
 In many schemes like Modi and then former Chief Minister Anandiben Patel's favorite health plan Mission Mangalam, the government puts people under contract which can be removed at any time
 inamen logon ko khud sarkaar hi 4000 se lekar 9000 tak alag
 Gives different salary
 iske alaava sarkaar bahari logon ko outsource karti he jo apane str par karmchaaree rakhte hai or unka bharpoor shoshan hota he
 The comments 2011 main kuch logon ne milakar gujarat hoicourt main is puri paddati ke khilaaf kanoonee ladaai ladi
 The High Court took a tough stance and canceled the Gujarat government's fixed salary system
 hoicourt ne apane aadesh main kaha ki maujuuda vyavastha nunatam vetan kaa bhi ulanghan karti he
 The government is obliged to pay a salary for a work
 ye bhi aadesh diya ki fiks tankhwaah niyam ke tahat bhartee sabhi karmchaariyon ko purnakalin sarkari grad diya janaa chahie
 Pravin says that the High Court has also warned the government that this policy is going to create corruption and exploit the youth, but the government challenged the decision in the Supreme Court, arguing that the financial burden on the government coffers, not obeying the order of the High Court 
 rajya main itane samay main kareeb 2 lakh se zyada logon kii bharti is niyam ke tahat hui he lekin ab tak unki maangen puri nahin kii gai hai
 In 2012, the Narendra Modi government went to the Supreme Court against the decision of Gujarat High Court where this case is still pending
 saatven vetan ayog ke lagu hone ke baad jab desh bhar main nunatam vetan 18000 rupee maheenaa ho chukaa he, lekin gujarat main kantrect par kaam karne vaale karmchaaree 9300 rupye masik tankhwaah par hi kaam kar rahe hai jabaki asaliyat main isse bhi kam miltaa he
 In 'vibrant Gujarat', the important issue of wage increase of these workers is being avoided without the fact that the matter is in the Supreme Court
 vetan badaye jane kii is maang ko lekar ahmedabad ke 6000 se zyada safaikarmi pichley ek saptaah se zyada samay se hadtaal par hai
 He says that full-time recruitment of many people happened long ago but the government is not giving them any attention
 kontract system kii vajah se unki haalat buree he
 After a long battle, the government has placed him on the government contract two years ago, which can be canceled anytime
 ye log sirf dihadi majdoor banakar rah gaye hai
 They do not get leave on Sunday also
 yahi nahin, agar biimaar pad gaye to us din kaa paisa gaya
 Narendra Modi has become the Prime Minister of the country, but the policies he made while being the Chief Minister of Gujarat, employees are still angry
 gitaben rathod naam kii karmchaaree yahaan tak kahati hai ki unhen mushkil se har maah 7000 se 8000 rupye tak mil paata he
 This too after working for more than 15 years
 kiraaye ke makaan main rahete hai, 3-4 hajaar kiraaya dete hai, bacchon kii padhai karaaen ki apana pet bharen
 They do not get medical nor Sunday leave
 yahi nahin, agar ghar main kisi kii maut ho jaae to bhi tankhwaah katwane kii naubat aati he
 Natwarbhai working in the Malaria Department of Ahmedabad Municipal Corporation has also been on strike for the past one week
 unki shikaayat he ki 20 saal kii naukari ke baavjood ve niyamit nahin kiye gaye, kontract par hi hai
 Salary is 9300 in total
 barsaat ke mausam main subah-shaam malaria prabhavit ilaaqon main chhidkaav main lage rahete hai lekin sehat ke liye koi beemaa nahin
 More than 200 posts in the Malaria Department have been vacant for the last 10 years
 magar unki tarah ke logon se kontract ke naam par shoshan ho rahaa he
 Vashistha Sharma is a teacher, not a cleaning employee
 shikshak bhi nahin, shiksha sahaayak
 The Gujarat government actually gives this status to its teachers
 paanch saal ke kontract par fiks selary main rakhti he
 Only after this, the salary of the entire teacher gets
 hair secondry main chemistry padhaane vaale vashisht sharma ko ek hi kaam ke liye alag-alag selary kii ye 'mistry' samaj main nahin aati
 Sharma says that he constantly listens to the Chief Minister and the Prime Minister on the issues of employment and minimum wages, who claim that the country has moved ahead
 lekin gujarat kaa shikshak yaa sarkari karmchaaree, jo tisare-chauthe varg main aata he uskaa ghar bhi chalaanaa mushkil he
 They say that suppose it is 15,000, then how will the house run
 unhen kuch lone bhi lenaa ho to bank kehete hai ki kam se kam 15,000 rupee tankhwaah honi chahie unhen to10 hajaar lone lene jaayen to wo bhi nahin mil saktaa
 In 1996, the government fixed salary for the first time in the Balguru scheme for primary teachers in Gujarat
 lekin narendra modi ke mukhyamantri banane ke baad 2006 main pehali baar gujarat main fiks tankhwaah kii niti bani
 Many posts came under its purview
 2006 main zyaadaatar padon ke liye tankhwaah 2500 rupye prati maah tay kii gai thi
 It was 4500 rupees for some posts
 baari virodh ke baavjood paanch saal yahi vetan chalata rahaa, 2011 main 2500 se tankhwaah badhaakar 4500 kii gai or 2012 main badhaakar 5300 rupye
 Ram Praveen of Jan Adhikar Manch, who is fighting against this government policy through legal and agitation, says that there are three types of recruitment and all three are exploited
 police main consteble, sab inspector, shikshak, patawaari jaise padon par 5 saal tak fiks selary rahati he
 These five years are neither counted in their jobs nor do they get any other government benefit
 seniority kaa laabh bhi nahin
 During this period, a long holiday cannot be taken
 modi or uske baad purv mukhyamantri anandiben patel kii chaheti swasthya yojana mishan mangalam jaisi kai yojanaon main sarkaar kontract ke tahat logon ko rakhti he jinhen kabhi bhi nikaala ja saktaa he
 Among them, the government itself varies from 4000 to 9000
 alag tankhwaah detii he
 Apart from this, the government outsources outsiders who keep staff at their level and are exploited to the fullest
 tippaniyan In 2011, some people fought a legal battle against this entire system in Gujarat High Court
 hoicourt ne kadaa rukh apanaaya or gujarat sarkaar ke is fiks tankhwaah system ko radd kar diya
 The High Court said in its order that the existing system also violates the minimum wage
 sarkaar ek kaam ke liye ek tankhwaah dene ke liye baadhya he
 It also ordered that full-time government grade should be given to all employees admitted under the fix salary rule
 praveen kehete hai ki sarkaar ko hoicourt ne chetavanee bhi di ki ye niti bhrashtachar paidaa karanevaali or yuvaaon kaa shoshan karanevaali he lekin sarkaar ne hoicourt ke aadesh ko na maanate hue sarkari tijori par aarthik boj padane kaa tark dete hue faisle ko supreme court main chunauti di
 Over 2 lakh people have been recruited under this rule in the state in this time, but till now their demands have not been met

 bhartiya raajnneeti is vakt buree tarah se uhapoh kaa shikaar he
 At the central level, there is complete uncertainty in governance
 lokapriy netaaon ke netritv main chal rahi rajya sarkaron main yah kshamta he ki ve bharat kii aarthik sambhaavna ko aage badha saken
 Given the possibility of a hung mandate at the Center in the future, the condition of the states will be the real mode of prosperity for Indian citizens
 acha content hameshaa tikaa rahata he
 The trends keep on coming
 film kisi bhi subject par ho, content main dam hoga to vah kamyaabi ke paaydaan chadhegi
 Here in recent years, the same has happened with some women oriented films
 jin filmon ne kamyaabi kaa swaad chakhaa, unka content acha tha
 She appealed to audiences in every way
 is vajah se ve achche cinema main tabdeel ho sakin
 If good films are made, they will succeed
 bollywood ko samaaj kaa aainaa kaha jaataa he
 The arrival and success of women-based films does not mean that our society has become sensitive about women, and has started showing sensitivity towards them
 is maamle main abhi lanbaa faasla tay karnaa he
 Whatever work is going on in the society about women, they are just a beginning
 filmein bhi usamen apane hisse kaa role nibhaane kii koshish kar rahi hai
 It is often said that films should be issue based
 meraa jor ishyus kii bajaae imoshans par, jajbaat par hota he
 Take the English Vinglish itself
 usamen maine language or english ko jariya banaaya
 Through it, the film tells the story of a man's confidence
 subject aisa hona chahie jo sabko apil kare, aam aadmi ko apane se jod sake
 Bollywood has a record that if it moves two steps forward, then it moves five steps backwards
 is record ko durust kiye jane kii jarurat he
 In recent years, the number of such films in Bollywood has increased, in which the female lead has been given the same solid role as the hero
 aise main yah kahana galat nahin hoga ki vimen oriented filmon ke din laute hai
 The decade of 1980-90 was a time when such films had completely disappeared from the scene
 tab sirf mardon vaali filmein hi banati thim
 Bollywood has also taken a turn with the changing times
 ab har saal nae sitare or diarectors kii nai jamaat hindi cinema se judati ja rahi he
 Because of this, new characters and new stories are constantly coming to the movies
 barfi (2012) main jhilmil chatarji baniin priyanka chopra ko hi len
 She was no less than Ranbir Kapoor in any sense
 cocktail (2012) main veronica ke role main deepika padukon ekadam alag or modern ladki kii tasviir pesh karti hai
 Deepika also competed with Shahrukh in Chennai Express (2013)
 pichley dinon ai hive (2014) main nai naveli aalia bhatta ne to apni acting se sabko hairat main hi daal diya
 He brought a sensitive subject closer to the hearts of the audience through his acting
 idhar, maradaani ko lekar bhi kaaphi kuch sunne ko mil rahaa he
 The whole picture is changing
 diarector or actor sensitive subjects ko chhu rahe hai or kuch sanjeeda kaam karne kii koshish kar rahe hai
 But one thing needs to be kept in mind about the film makers: We are not social activists, we are storytellers, storytellers
 ham jo bhi film banaate hai, usamen bijness factor bhi rahata he
 So our effort is to make complete films
 sari jimmedaari film industry ke kandhon par hi nahin honi chahie
 We can just try to make good movies
 socity ke alag-alag tabakon kaa bhi ferj banataa he ki ve mahilaon or unase jude ishyus ko lekar aawaaj uthaaen
 a positive start is possible with all-round effort
 hamaari filmein international film awadrs main bahut kam jagah bana paati hai
 With this, their standard is estimated
 lagaan ko chhod den to or kisi film kaa naam dhyaan main hi nahin aata, jiske naam aisi uplabdhi darj ho
 One more important thing, we have more emphasis on quality than quality
 saal bhar main 500 se zyada filmein relies ho jaati hai lekin unamem se yaad ikkaa-dukka hi rahati hai
 This trend has to change
 sirf profit or ginati ke paimaane par filmein banane se kahani gaun ho jaati he
 If the film will be good and the content will be solid, then the films themselves will pull the audience to theaters and rain the money
 samay-samay par mahilaon ko lekar yaadgaar filmein banaai jaati rahi hai, jinamein nargis kii madar india (1957), jaya bhadudi kii guddi (1971) or mili (1975), minaa kumari kii pakija (1972), rekha kii umrao jaan (1981), manisha koirala kii bombai (1995) or kaajol kii dilavaale dulahaniya le jaaenge (1995) aisi hi filmein hai
 In this episode, if we look at the films after 2000, Tabu's Chandni Bar (2001) and Chini Kam (2007), Vidya Balan's Parineeta (2005), Paa (2009) and Kahaani (2012) and my film starring Sridevi The English Vinglish (2012) can be placed
 ye ve filmein hai, jinhone aurat ke puure stregal or puri shakhsiyat ko damdaar andaaj main pesh kiya
 Here in three-four years, the female actors and their films are telling in gestures how the journey will be going forward
 ye actors parade par tarah-tarah ke kirdaar nibhaa rahi hai
 She is getting ahead of the feeling of being just a woman, living life in her own way
 ek majubat police afasar parade par najar aati he to ek ladki akele honeymoon par nikal jaati he
 a girl raises her voice against her exploitation
 yani auraton ke liye aise kirdaar gadhe ja rahe hai, jo asal jindagi ke kareeb hai
 Overall, the thinking of film makers is changing
 ab auraten sirf sho-pis kii tarah filmon main nahin aatin, balki unhone apana vajood hasil kar liya he
